The cleanliness of the guest room needs to be improved. The marble bedside table has visible stains, the switch is covered with dust, and the sofa is not very clean. 3. The decoration of the bathroom is poor, and the price of the executive room is twice as expensive. I thought it would be better, and it is estimated to be similar to the ordinary room. Advantages 1. The breakfast is good 2. The location is not bad and it is convenient to do things 3. The young man in the lobby is very nice and diligent. , to no avail.
